## This Week in Security: Your News Briefing

Welcome to your weekly security roundup. We've tracked down the **10 most important stories** this
week‚Äîthe ones everyone's talking about, from critical threats to emerging trends that could shape
your security posture. Leading the news this week is **Appsec Roundup - June 2024**, which has
sparked conversation across 9 sources. Meanwhile, the industry is closely tracking **Secure by
Design roundup - April 2024** with 6 mentions, along with emerging details on **CVE-2026-2962 |
D-Link DWR-M960 1.01.07 Scheduled Reboot...**, **CVE-2025-49113**, and **CVE-2026-2981 | UTT HiPER
810G up to 1.7.7-1711...**. Here's the full breakdown of what you need to know.

### üö® Critical Threats This Week

First, the stories that demand your immediate attention:

**1. Appsec Roundup - June 2024**
   Mentioned across 9 industry sources this week. The most important stories around threat modeling, appsec and secure by design for June, 2024.
   [Get the details ‚Üí](https://shostack.org/blog/appsec-roundup-june-2024/)

**2. CVE-2026-2962 | D-Link DWR-M960 1.01.07 Scheduled Reboot Configuration Endpoint /boafrm/formDateReboot sub_460F30 submit-url stack-based overflow**
   Mentioned across 6 industry sources this week. A vulnerability, which was classified as critical , was found in D-Link DWR-M960 1.
   [Get the details ‚Üí](https://nvd.nist.gov/vuln/detail/CVE-2026-2962)

**3. CVE-2025-49113**
   Mentioned across 3 industry sources this week. Currently trending CVE - Hype Score: 9 - Roundcube Webmail before 1.
   [Get the details ‚Üí](https://nvd.nist.gov/vuln/detail/CVE-2025-49113)

### üõ†Ô∏è Tools, Updates & Releases

New capabilities and releases worth knowing about:

**1. Secure by Design roundup - April 2024**
   A less busy month in appsec, AI, and regulation, but still interesting stories. Referenced in 6 stories this week.
   [Explore ‚Üí](https://shostack.org/blog/appsec-roundup-april-2024/)

**2. Promoting AI Security ‚Äî Acting Assistant Privacy Commissioner Speaks at the GenA.I. Symposium**
   . Referenced in 2 stories this week.
   [Explore ‚Üí](http://www.pcpd.org.hk/english/whatsnew/20251031.html)

**3. Security Affairs newsletter Round 564 by Pierluigi Paganini ‚Äì INTERNATIONAL EDITION**
   A new round of the weekly Security Affairs newsletter has arrived! Every week, the best security art. Referenced in 2 stories this week.
   [Explore ‚Üí](https://securityaffairs.com/188332/breaking-news/security-affairs-newsletter-round-564-by-pierluigi-paganini-international-edition.html)

### What You Should Do Next

**Monitor these** in your environment next week:
- Any new CVE announcements related to systems you operate
- Emerging attack techniques being discussed in the community
- Updates and patches for tools your team uses

**Have a look at** the full deep-dives in the trending stories below. Each one provides context that could inform your security decisions this week.
